it\n\t\t\t\tbtn.click();\n\t\t\t\tevent.keyCode = 0\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\t\n\tfunction getCheckedRadio(ctl) {\n        var radioButtons = document.getElementsByName(ctl);\n        for (var x = 0; x < radioButtons.length; x++) {if (radioButtons[x].checked) { return radioButtons[x].value; }}\n\t\t}\n      \n    function getDropDown(ctl)\t{\n\t\tvar ele = return true; } \n\t\t}\n\n\tfunction searchSite(queryCtl, imgCtl, artistCtl, frM, frD, frY, todM, todD, todY, scopeCtl)\t{\n\t\t//searchstr = String.Format(searchstr, txtQuery.ClientID,
